  da(cz, s, ci, dd, dn, dn, q, cj, bool);
  s element();
  dd t();
  q dh();
};
template <class db> struct di { using dj = typename db::dk::v; };
namespace h {
template <int> struct dl {};
template <typename w> class IteratorRange {
public:
  typedef w dm;
  dm begin();
  dm end();
};
template <typename GV, int codim>
auto entities(GV gv, dl<codim>)
    -> IteratorRange<decltype(gv.template begin<codim>())>;
template <typename GV> auto elements(GV gv) -> decltype(entities(gv, dl<0>()));
template <class ViewTraits> class db {
public:
  typedef ViewTraits Traits;
  typedef typename Traits ::dk dk;
  template <int cd> struct dl {
    typedef typename Traits ::dl<cd>::w w;
    typedef typename Traits ::dl<cd>::y y;
  };
  template <int cd> typename dl<cd>::w begin();
};
template <class> struct DefaultLevelGridViewTraits;
template <class x> struct DefaultLeafGridViewTraits {
  typedef x cg;
  typedef typename cg ::Traits ::LeafIndexSet dk;
  template <int cd> struct dl {
    typedef typename cg ::Traits ::dl<cd>::Partition<dg>::LeafIterator w;
    typedef typename cg ::dl<cd> y;
  };
};
template <int, class> class EntityIterator;
class dk;
template <class GridFamily> class cg {
public:
  typedef typename GridFamily::Traits::LeafGridView LeafGridView;
  template <int> struct dl {};
};
template <class GridFamily>
class GridDefaultImplementation : public cg<GridFamily> {
public:
  typedef typename GridFamily::Traits Traits;
};
template <int, int, class x, template <int, int, class> class,
          template <int, int, class> class, template <int, df, class> class,
          template <class> class, template <class> class,
          template <class> class, template <class> class,
          template <class> class, template <int, df, class> class, class, class,
          class, class, class, class, class, template <class> class,
          template <class> class LeafGridViewTraits,
          template <int, class> class>
struct GridTraits {
  template <int cd> struct dl {
    template <int> struct Partition {
      typedef EntityIterator<cd, x> LeafIterator;
    };
  };
  typedef db<LeafGridViewTraits<x>> LeafGridView;
  typedef dk LeafIndexSet;
};
template <int codim, class cg> class EntityIterator {
public:
  void operator++();
  typename cg::dl<codim> operator*();
  bool operator!=(EntityIterator);
};
class dk {
public:
  typedef int v;
};
template <int, class> class YaspGrid;
template <int, int, class> class YaspEntity;
template <int, class> class YaspEntitySeed;
template <class> class YaspIntersectionIterator;
template <class> class YaspIntersection;
template <class> class YaspHierarchicIterator;
template <class> class YaspGlobalIdSet;
template <int, int, class> class YaspGeometry;
template <int, int, class> class YaspLevelIterator;
template <class, int> class YaspIndexSet;
template <int dim, class Coordinates> struct YaspGridFamily {
  typedef GridTraits<
      dim, dim, YaspGrid<dim, Coordinates>, YaspGeometry, YaspEntity,
      YaspLevelIterator, YaspIntersection, YaspIntersection,
      YaspIntersectionIterator, YaspIntersectionIterator,
      YaspHierarchicIterator, YaspLevelIterator,
      YaspIndexSet<YaspGrid<dim, Coordinates>, false>,
      YaspIndexSet<YaspGrid<dim, Coordinates>, true>,
      YaspGlobalIdSet<YaspGrid<dim, Coordinates>>, bigunsignedint<dim>,
      YaspGlobalIdSet<YaspGrid<dim, Coordinates>>, bigunsignedint<dim>, int,
      DefaultLevelGridViewTraits, DefaultLeafGridViewTraits, YaspEntitySeed>
      Traits;
};
template <int dim, class = int>
class YaspGrid : public GridDefaultImplementation<YaspGridFamily<dim, int>> {};
} // namespace h
template <template <long> class bp, class Indices>
struct MultiDomainTupleSharedPtrConst {
  template <long i> using PtrType = std::ax<bp<i>>;
  using ab = typename cy<std::al, PtrType, Indices>::ab;
};
template <template <long> class SubDomainTypeTag, int i>
struct SubDomainFVGridGeometryImpl {
  using ab = p<SubDomainTypeTag<i>, bx::cl>;
};
template <template <long> class SubDomainTypeTag, int i>
struct SubDomainGridVariablesImpl {
  using ab = p<SubDomainTypeTag<i>, bx::cw>;
};
template <template <long> class SubDomainTypeTag, int i>
struct SubDomainSolutionVectorImpl {
  using ab = p<SubDomainTypeTag<i>, bx::ci>;
};
template <typename... SubDomainTypeTags> struct StaggeredMultiDomainTraits {
  static constexpr long numSubDomains = sizeof...(SubDomainTypeTags);
  template <long id>
  using SubDomainTypeTag = std::aj<id, std::al<SubDomainTypeTags...>>;
  using Indices = std::ar<numSubDomains>;
  template <long id>
  using SubDomainSolutionVector =
      typename SubDomainSolutionVectorImpl<SubDomainTypeTag, id>::ab;
  template <int id> struct SubDomain {
    using cl = typename SubDomainFVGridGeometryImpl<SubDomainTypeTag, id>::ab;
    using cw = typename SubDomainGridVariablesImpl<SubDomainTypeTag, id>::ab;
  };
  using ci = typename cy<h::cr, SubDomainSolutionVector, Indices>::ab;
  template <template <long> class bp>
  using TupleOfSharedPtrConst =
      typename MultiDomainTupleSharedPtrConst<bp, Indices>::ab;
};
template <int id, class z, class cz>
class SubDomainCCLocalAssemblerBase : da<z, cz> {
  using ParentType = da<z, cz>;
  using ci = typename cz::ci;
  using SubSolutionVector = p<z, bx::ci>;
  using cw = p<z, bx::cw>;
  using cl = typename cw::cl;
  using db = typename cl::db;
  using s = typename db::dl<0>::y;
  using CouplingManager = typename cz::CouplingManager;
public:
  static auto domainId = h::bm<id>();
  SubDomainCCLocalAssemblerBase(cz assembler, s element, ci curSol,
                                CouplingManager couplingManager)
      : ParentType(
            assembler, element, curSol,
            localView(assembler.gridGeometry(domainId)), 0, 0,
            localView(assembler.gridVariables(domainId).gridFluxVarsCache()),
            domainId, couplingManager) {}
  void assembleResidual(SubSolutionVector) {
    auto element = this->element(), t = this->t(), dh = this->dh();
    dh.bind(element, t, 0);
  }
};
template <unsigned long, class, class, bool> class SubDomainCCLocalAssembler;
template <unsigned long id, class z, class cz>
class SubDomainCCLocalAssembler<id, z, cz, true>
    : public SubDomainCCLocalAssemblerBase<id, z, cz> {
  using ParentType = SubDomainCCLocalAssemblerBase<id, z, cz>;
  ParentType::ParentType;
};
template <class MDTraits, bool useImplicitAssembly = true>
class MultiDomainFVAssembler {
  template <long id> using SubDomainTypeTag = typename MDTraits::SubDomain<id>;
public:
  template <long id> using cj = p<SubDomainTypeTag<id>, bx::cj>;
  template <long id> using cw = typename MDTraits::SubDomain<id>::cw;
  template <long id> using cl = typename MDTraits::SubDomain<id>::cl;
  using ci = typename MDTraits::ci;
  using dc = ci;
  using CouplingManager = int;
  static constexpr bool isImplicit() { return useImplicitAssembly; }
  using GridGeometryTuple = typename MDTraits::TupleOfSharedPtrConst<cl>;
  using ThisType = MultiDomainFVAssembler;
  template <int id> struct SubDomainAssemblerType {
    using ab = SubDomainCCLocalAssembler<id, SubDomainTypeTag<id>, ThisType,
                                         isImplicit()>;
  };
  template <long id>
  using SubDomainAssembler = typename SubDomainAssemblerType<id>::ab;
  void assembleResidual(ci curSol) { assembleResidual(*residual_, curSol); }
  void assembleResidual(dc r, ci curSol) {
    using namespace h::bn;
    bu(r,
       [&](auto domainId) { assembleResidual_(domainId, domainId, curSol); });
  }
  template <unsigned long i> auto gridGeometry(h::bm<i> domainId) {
    return *std::au<domainId>(gridGeometryTuple_);
  }
  template <unsigned long i> auto gridView(h::bm<i> domainId) {
    return gridGeometry(domainId).gridView();
  }
  template <unsigned long i> cw<i> gridVariables(h::bm<i>);
  std::ax<CouplingManager> couplingManager_;
  template <unsigned long i, class SubRes>
  void assembleResidual_(h::bm<i> domainId, SubRes subRes, ci curSol) {
    assemble_(domainId, [&](auto element) {
      SubDomainAssembler<i> subDomainAssembler(*this, element, curSol,
                                               *couplingManager_);
      subDomainAssembler.assembleResidual(subRes);
    });
  }
  template <unsigned long i, class AssembleElementFunc>
  void assemble_(h::bm<i> domainId, AssembleElementFunc assembleElement) {
    auto __trans_tmp_2 = gridView(domainId);
    for (auto element : elements(__trans_tmp_2))
      assembleElement(element);
  }
  GridGeometryTuple gridGeometryTuple_;
  std::ax<ci> residual_;
};
template <class> class PDESolver {
public:
  MultiDomainFVAssembler<StaggeredMultiDomainTraits<int>> assembler();
};
template <class cz> class NewtonSolver : PDESolver<cz> {
  using ci = typename cz::dc;
  ci newtonBegin_u;
  virtual void newtonBegin() {
    this->assembler().assembleResidual(newtonBegin_u);
  }
  std::aw partialReassembler_;
};
template <class cz> class MultiDomainNewtonSolver : NewtonSolver<cz> {
public:
  MultiDomainNewtonSolver(std::ax<cz>, std::ax<int>, std::ax<int>);
};
template <class> class FicksLawImplementation;
template <class GG, class GFVC> class FVGridVariables {
public:
  using cl = GG;
  using cs = GFVC;
  cs gridFluxVarsCache();
};

  using GG = p<z, cl>;
  using GFVC = p<z, cs>;
  using ab = FVGridVariables<GG, GFVC>;
};
template <class z> struct ci<z, int> { using ab = int; };

template <class GridCache> typename GridCache::de localView(GridCache);
template <class GV> class BaseGridGeometry {
  using GridIndexType = typename di<GV>::dj;
  using s = typename GV::dl<0>::y;
public:
  using db = GV;
  db gridView();
  s element(GridIndexType);
};
template <class cl> class CCSimpleConnectivityMap {
  using db = typename cl::db;
  using GridIndexType = typename di<db>::dj;
  struct DataJ {
    GridIndexType globalJ;
    h::cv scvfsJ;
  };
public:
  std::av<DataJ> operator[](GridIndexType);
};
template <class GG> class CCTpfaFVElementGeometry {
public:
  using SubControlVolumeFace = typename GG::SubControlVolumeFace;
  using cl = GG;
  cl gridGeometry();
};
struct CCTpfaDefaultGridGeometryTraits {
  using SubControlVolumeFace = int;
  template <class cl> using ConnectivityMap = CCSimpleConnectivityMap<cl>;
  template <class cl, bool> using de = CCTpfaFVElementGeometry<cl>;
};
template <class, bool, class = CCTpfaDefaultGridGeometryTraits>
class CCTpfaFVGridGeometry;
template <class GV, class Traits>
class CCTpfaFVGridGeometry<GV, false, Traits> : public BaseGridGeometry<GV> {
  using ThisType = CCTpfaFVGridGeometry;
  using ConnectivityMap = typename Traits::ConnectivityMap<ThisType>;
public:
  using de = typename Traits::de<ThisType, false>;
  using SubControlVolumeFace = typename Traits::SubControlVolumeFace;
  ConnectivityMap connectivityMap();
};
template <class Traits> class CCGridVolumeVariables {
  using ThisType = CCGridVolumeVariables;
public:
  static constexpr bool cachingEnabled = false;
  using de = typename Traits::de<ThisType, cachingEnabled>;
};
struct CCTpfaDefaultGridVolumeVariablesTraits {
  template <class, bool> using de = int;
};
template <class GFVC> class CCTpfaElementFluxVariablesCache {
  using cn = typename GFVC::Traits::cn;
public:
  using cm = typename GFVC::cm;
  template <class dd, class dn>
  void bind(typename dd::cl::db::dl<0>::y, dd t, dn elemVolVars) {
    auto gridGeometry = t.gridGeometry(),
         connectivityMapI = gridGeometry.connectivityMap()[0],
         elementJ = gridGeometry.element(connectivityMapI[0].globalJ);
    cn filler(0);
    for (auto scvfIdx : connectivityMapI[0].scvfsJ) {
      auto scvfJ(scvfIdx);
      filler.fill(this, fluxVarsCache_[0], elementJ, t, elemVolVars, scvfJ);
    }
  }
  std::av<cm> fluxVarsCache_;
};
template <class FVC, class FVCF> struct CCTpfaDefaultGridFVCTraits {
  using cm = FVC;
  using cn = FVCF;
  template <class cs, bool> using de = CCTpfaElementFluxVariablesCache<cs>;
};
template <class cm, class cn, bool, class = CCTpfaDefaultGridFVCTraits<cm, cn>>
class CCTpfaGridFluxVariablesCache;
template <class FVC, class FVCF, class TheTraits>
class CCTpfaGridFluxVariablesCache<FVC, FVCF, false, TheTraits> {
  using ThisType = CCTpfaGridFluxVariablesCache;
public:
  using Traits = TheTraits;
  using cm = typename Traits::cm;
  static constexpr bool cachingEnabled = false;
  using de = typename Traits::de<ThisType, cachingEnabled>;
};
namespace bx {

  using db = typename p<z, cg>::LeafGridView;
  using ab = CCTpfaFVGridGeometry<db, 0>;

  using ab = CCGridVolumeVariables<CCTpfaDefaultGridVolumeVariablesTraits>;
};
template <class z> struct cs<z, int> {
  using cm = p<z, cm>;
  using cn = p<z, cn>;
  using ab = CCTpfaGridFluxVariablesCache<cm, cn, 0>;
};
template <class z> struct cf<z, int> { using ab = double; };

template <class> class PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheImplementation;
template <class z>
using PorousMediumFluxVariablesCache =
    PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheImplementation<z>;
template <class z> class DiffusionCacheChooser : public p<z, bx::cx>::Cache {};
template <class z>
class PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheImplementation
    : public DiffusionCacheChooser<z> {};
template <class> class PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheFillerImplementation;
template <class z>
using PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheFiller =
    PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheFillerImplementation<z>;
template <class z> class PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheFillerImplementation {
  using ch = p<z, bx::ch>;
  using db = typename p<z, bx::cl>::db;
  using dd = typename p<z, bx::cl>::de;
  using SubControlVolumeFace = typename dd::SubControlVolumeFace;
  using dn = typename p<z, bx::cp>::de;
  using s = typename db::dl<0>::y;
public:
  PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheFillerImplementation(ch);
  template <class FluxVariablesCacheContainer, class cm>
  void fill(FluxVariablesCacheContainer, cm scvfFluxVarsCache, s element, dd t,
            dn elemVolVars, SubControlVolumeFace scvf) {
    using DiffusionType = p<z, bx::cx>;
    using DiffusionFiller = typename DiffusionType::Cache::Filler;
    DiffusionFiller::fill(scvfFluxVarsCache, 0, 0, 0, element, t, elemVolVars,
                          scvf, this);
  }
};
template <class z> using FicksLaw = FicksLawImplementation<z>;
template <class z> class FicksLawImplementation {
  using cf = p<z, bx::cf>;
  using ch = p<z, bx::ch>;
  using dd = typename p<z, bx::cl>::de;
  using SubControlVolumeFace = typename dd::SubControlVolumeFace;
  using db = typename p<z, bx::cl>::db;
  using dn = typename p<z, bx::cp>::de;
  using s = typename db::dl<0>::y;
  using cm = p<z, bx::cm>;
  using cq = p<z, bx::cq>;
  class TpfaFicksLawCacheFiller {
  public:
    template <class cn>
    static void fill(cm scvfFluxVarsCache, int phaseIdx, int compIdx,
                     ch problem, s element, dd t, dn elemVolVars,
                     SubControlVolumeFace scvf, cn) {
      scvfFluxVarsCache.updateDiffusion(problem, element, t, elemVolVars, scvf,
                                        phaseIdx, compIdx);
    }
  };
  class TpfaFicksLawCache {
  public:
    using Filler = TpfaFicksLawCacheFiller;
    void updateDiffusion(ch, s, dd, dn, SubControlVolumeFace, int, int) {
      calculateTransmissibility;
    }
  };
public:
  using Cache = TpfaFicksLawCache;
  static cf calculateTransmissibility() {
    [](auto) {
      if constexpr (cq::isTracerFluidSystem())
        ;
    };
  }
};
namespace bx {
template <class z> struct cm<z, int> {
  using ab = PorousMediumFluxVariablesCache<z>;
};
template <class z> struct cn<z, int> {
  using ab = PorousMediumFluxVariablesCacheFiller<z>;
};
template <class z> struct cx<z, int> { using ab = FicksLaw<z>; };
template <class z> struct cj<z, int> { using ab = z; };
} // namespace bx
class Base {
  static bool isTracerFluidSystem();
};
namespace bx {
template <class z> struct ch<z, int> { using ab = int; };
template <class z> struct cq<z, int> { using ab = Base; };
template <class z> struct cg<z, int> { using ab = h::YaspGrid<2>; };
} // namespace bx
main() try {
  using DarcyTypeTag = int;
  using Traits = StaggeredMultiDomainTraits<DarcyTypeTag>;
  using CouplingManager = int;
  auto couplingManager = std::az<CouplingManager>(),
       linearSolver = std::az<int>();
  using cz = MultiDomainFVAssembler<Traits>;
  auto assembler = std::az<cz>();
  using NewtonSolver = MultiDomainNewtonSolver<cz>;
  NewtonSolver(assembler, linearSolver, couplingManager);
} catch (int) {
}
